1. 영어 Word2Vec 학습시키기¶

In [1]:
import urllib.request
import zipfile
import re
import nltk
from nltk.tokenize import word_tokenize, sent_tokenize
from lxml import etree

1) 훈련 데이터 이해하기¶

In [2]:
#  
urllib.request.urlretrieve("https://raw.githubusercontent.com/GaoleMeng/RNN-and-FFNN-textClassification/master/ted_en-20160408.xml", filename="ted_en-20160408.xml")
Out[2]:
('ted_en-20160408.xml', <http.client.HTTPMessage at 0x1153b9ef0>)

2) 훈련 데이터 전처리하기¶

In [3]:
targetXML = open('ted_en-20160408.xml', 'r', encoding='UTF8') #   
target_text = etree.parse(targetXML) #  
parse_text = '\n'.join(target_text.xpath('//content/text()')) # xml  <content> </content>
In [4]:
#   (Audio), (Laughter)    
content_text = re.sub(r'\([^)]*\)', '', parse_text)
In [5]:
#     
sent_text = sent_tokenize(content_text)
In [6]:
#     ,   
normalized_text = []
for string in sent_text:
    tokens = re.sub(r"[^a-z0-9]+", " ", string.lower())
    normalized_text.append(tokens)
In [7]:
#      
result = []
result = [word_tokenize(sentence) for sentence in normalized_text]
In [8]:
#   
print('   : {}'.format(len(result)))

   : 273424
In [9]:
#  3  
for line in result[:3]:
    print(line)

['here', 'are', 'two', 'reasons', 'companies', 'fail', 'they', 'only', 'do', 'more', 'of', 'the', 'same', 'or', 'they', 'only', 'do', 'what', 's', 'new']
['to', 'me', 'the', 'real', 'real', 'solution', 'to', 'quality', 'growth', 'is', 'figuring', 'out', 'the', 'balance', 'between', 'two', 'activities', 'exploration', 'and', 'exploitation']
['both', 'are', 'necessary', 'but', 'it', 'can', 'be', 'too', 'much', 'of', 'a', 'good', 'thing']

3) Word2Vec 훈련시키기¶

gensim.models Word2Vec .

  • size : ( )
  • window : context window size
  • min_count : ( X)
  • workers :
  • sg : 0 CBOW, 1 Skip-gram
In [10]:
from gensim.models import Word2Vec
In [11]:
# Word2Vec 
model = Word2Vec(sentences=result, size=100, window=5, min_count=5, workers=4, sg=0)
In [12]:
# 
model_result = model.wv.most_similar("man")
print(model_result)

[('woman', 0.8504765033721924), ('guy', 0.8242725133895874), ('lady', 0.79554283618927), ('girl', 0.7617751359939575), ('boy', 0.7551615238189697), ('soldier', 0.7291037440299988), ('gentleman', 0.7116379141807556), ('kid', 0.6900016069412231), ('friend', 0.6854373812675476), ('poet', 0.6748146414756775)]

4) Word2Vec 모델 저장하고 로드하기¶

In [13]:
#  
model.wv.save_word2vec_format('./eng_w2v')
In [14]:
#  
from gensim.models import KeyedVectors
loaded_model = KeyedVectors.load_word2vec_format("eng_w2v")
In [15]:
# 
model_result = loaded_model.most_similar("man")
print(model_result)

5) 임베딩 벡터 시각화 하기¶

2. 파이토치(PyTorch)의 nn.Embedding()¶

. (embedding layer) train (pre-trained word embedding) . nn.Embedding() .

In [16]:
train_data = 'you need to know how to code'
word_set = set(train_data.split()) #     
vocab = {tkn: i+2 for i, tkn in enumerate(word_set)}  #      
vocab['<unk>'] = 0
vocab['<pad>'] = 1

torch nn.Embedding .

  • num_embeddings : ( )
  • embedding_dim :
  • padding_idx : (optional)
In [17]:
import torch.nn as nn
embedding_layer = nn.Embedding(num_embeddings=len(vocab), #     =>   
                               embedding_dim=3, #    
                               padding_idx=1)
In [18]:
print(embedding_layer.weight)

3.1 IMDB 리뷰 데이터를 훈련 데이터로 사용하기¶

. IMDB .

In [19]:
from torchtext import data, datasets
In [20]:
# Field  
TEXT = data.Field(sequential=True, batch_first=True, lower=True)
LABEL = data.Field(sequential=False, batch_first=True)
